<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаливать.html>отча́ливать</a> (26763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчалить.html>отча́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otčálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><i>нареч.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаянный.html>отча́янный</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"> — <a href = vnd.unilang:ой.html>Ой́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ой.html>ой́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ой.html>ой́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ой.html>ой́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шайте</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> щиплетесь? — <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаянный.html>отча́янно</a></span> запищал <a href = vnd.unilang:тоненький.html>то́ненький</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голосок.html>голосо́к</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9,_%D0%90%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B5%D0%B9_%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Толстой, Алексей Николаевич">A. Н. <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a></a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>Золото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключик.html>клю́чик</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приключение.html>Приключе́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:буратино.html>Буратино</a>, <span class="example-date">1935</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a>.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otčájanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаянный.html>отча́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčájannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>desperate</li>
<li>foolhardy, reckless</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rotten, frightful, awful</li></ol>

***отчаяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяться.html>отча́яться</a> (10796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаять.html>ча́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяться.html>отча́яться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčájatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаиваться.html>отча́иваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to despair, to be in despair</li>
<li>to not to hope, to lose hope <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяться.html>отча́яться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́го</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otčájatʹsja</b> spastí bolʹnóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">despair of the patient's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяться.html>отча́ялся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снова.html>сно́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́деть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja užé <b>otčájalsja</b> snóva uvídetʹ vas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I didn't hope to see you again; I'd lost (all) hope of seeing you again</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***отчего.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчего.html>отчего</a> (1655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from, out of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, genitive singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчего.html>отчего́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčevó</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative adverb</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> why? <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">from what cause</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The answer begins with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оттого.html>оттого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ottovó što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отчего́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otčevó-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>че<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, местоименное, <a href = vnd.unilang:вопросительный.html>вопроси́тельное</a>, обстоятельственное, <a href = vnd.unilang:причина.html>причи́ны</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́з</a>; неизменяемое.

</p>

***отчизна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчизна.html>отчи́зна</a> (18334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">отьчизна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otĭčizna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(fore)fathers, lineage, patrimony</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">вітчи́зна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vitčýzna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-изна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-izna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчизна.html>отчи́зна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčízna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчизна.html>отчи́зны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчизна.html>отчи́зны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчизна.html>отчи́зн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fatherland, motherland, homeland, home country</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́чество</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otéčestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дина</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rodina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи́з<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчий.html>о́тчий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótčij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fatherly, paternal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчий.html>о́тчий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелу́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ótčij</b> pocelúj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>paternal</b> kiss</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> native
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчий.html>о́тчий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>край</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ótčij</b> kraj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>father</b>land</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:числить.html>чи́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">číslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислить.html>отчи́слить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčíslitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислять.html>отчисля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deduct</li>
<li>to assign, to allot</li>
<li>to remit, to transfer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислить.html>отчи́слить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бюджет.html>бюдже́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otčíslitʹ</b> srédstva v bjudžét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay/remit funds to the (government) budget</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dismiss, to expel, to send down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислить.html>отчи́слить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otčíslitʹ</b> v zapás</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to transfer to the reserve</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислить.html>отчи́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otčíslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислять.html>отчисля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčisljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислить.html>отчи́слить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deduct</li>
<li>to assign, to allot</li>
<li>to remit, to transfer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислять.html>отчисля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бюджет.html>бюдже́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otčisljátʹ</b> srédstva v bjudžét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay/remit funds to the (government) budget</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dismiss, to expel, to send down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчислять.html>отчисля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otčisljátʹ</b> v zapás</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to transfer to the reserve</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***отчитываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчитываться.html>отчи́тываться</a> (18210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчитываться.html>отчи́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčítyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчитаться.html>отчита́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to report, to give a report</li>
<li>to give an account
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отчитываться.html>отчи́тываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otčítyvatʹsja</b> v čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give an account of something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***отчудить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчудить.html>отчуди́ть</a> (18664)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чуд-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čud-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The middle part is cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čužój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">another's, alien</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but lacking the Early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-jь</i> suffix, suggesting that the term originated in Early Proto Slavic or before.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчудить.html>отчуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otčudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отчужда́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to alienate, to expropriate</li>
<li>to estrange</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do something very strange</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:чу.html>чу</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
